redman
03-24-2007, 16:06
http://img124.imageshack.us/img124/710/uo0303gg0.jpg
As you wanted

and LostraC here is the script I made by myself:

onGMpause
setLoot D7 0B
setMeleeKill orc
setMeleeKill orc spearman
setMeleeKill orc shaman
setMeleeKill snake
move 33057,32047,8
move 33057,32018,8
move 33072,32016,8
move 33046,32030,8
move 33045,32030,9
move 33058,32047,9
move 33055,32020,9
move 33056,32029,8
move 33057,32028,7
move 33059,32027,7
move 33055,32029,8
gotoScriptLine 0

enough food to heal yourself and it kills shaman only if someone ropes/you fall down into a hole. There is no waypoint that goes to shaman/quest room

Edit: 7k/h there for me :)

07:58 Your position is : 32366,31058,7 < dog sled
07:59 Your position is : 32471,31095,7 < nearby igloo where you'll start this script


onGMpause
setAny
setMeleeKill rat
setMeleeKill Winter Wolf
setMeleeKill Penguin
setMeleeKill Chakoya Tribewarden
setMeleeKill Chakoya Windcaller
setMeleeKill Chakoya Toolshaper
setMeleeKill polar bear
setPriority Chakoya Windcaller:+1
setLoot D7 0B
setLoot D5 1C
setLoot 08 17
#shard
setLoot 7A 1C
move 32481,31089,9
move 32445,31075,9
move 32492,31054,9
move 32504,31073,9

sayMessage exiva > 82 2B 7E 9C 79 07 EB 1A 01 09
move 32299,31134,7
:hi
sayMessage hi
#to give the NPC time to actually greet you.
waitX 2
IfTrue ($lastmsg$#string=#Greetings stranger.) Goto $nlineoflabel:deposit$
waitX 5
:wait
IfTrue ($lastmsg$#string=#Good bye.) Goto $nlineoflabel:hi$
IfTrue ($lastmsg$#string=#<sarcastic> AND GOOD BYE TO YOU TOO!) Goto $nlineoflabel:hi$
#to loop the IfTrues to see if the NPC has said bye to the last player
gotoScriptLine $nlineoflabel:wait$
:deposit
sayMessage deposit $countitems:D7 0B$
waitX 1
sayMessage yes
waitX 1
sayMessage bye
#back to hunt

Shortened the quote.

At first gratz to the levels and the 2k posts ofc.

2nd.
I am pretty sure that you can get it in 2-3 daysby pging a mage like this:
First get the level for making avalanches.
(already in minos)
Then when you once got it (was it 28 or 32??)
Make 1-2 bps of avalanches via mana potions.
Waste them on the dara minos when full spawn.
Collect the loot in a loot bag.
Sell the loot when ur out of runes.
Get new manas for runeburning and repeat it.

and speacially in your rich guy case:
get a friend to block for you till the level for avas.
Make them with cash from ur ek.
Pwn the minos.
Only pick up gps or even nothing.
Wait for spawn.

Or
Log ur mage at the mino spawn.
Exp ur knight.
Logg off from time to time and pwn the tower.
Log back to ur mage and reapeat it.
